# Grand Army of the Republic

[Edit](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic?veaction=edit) 

* [Edit source](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic?action=edit)
* [History](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic?action=history)
* [Purge](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic?action=purge)
* [Talk (28)](/wiki/Talk:Grand_Army_of_the_Republic)

[![This article details a subject that is considered canon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "This article details a subject that is considered canon.")

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [This article covers the Canon version of this subject.](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "This article covers the Canon version of this subject.") |  | [Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic/Legends "Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.") |  |

[![OnACanonArticle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "Canon")[![GoToLegends](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic/Legends "Grand Army of the Republic/Legends")

This article is about **the army used by the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars")**. You may be looking for **the [Republic army](/wiki/Republic_army "Republic army") used early in the Galactic Republic's founding, or the [army](/wiki/New_Republic_army "New Republic army") used by the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic")**.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

## Other information

### Affiliation

* [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic")[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)
  + [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military")[[14]](#cite_note-Catalyst-14)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Military_unit)

:   "*As my first act with this new authority, I will create a Grand Army of the Republic to counter the increasing threats of the Separatists.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

The **Grand Army of the Republic** (**GAR**), also known as the **Great Army of the Republic**, the **Republic Army**, the **Grand Army**, the **Galactic Army**, or simply the **clone army**, was the [army](/wiki/Army "Army") branch of the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") throughout the duration of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). At the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") activated hundreds of thousands of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") to fight the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). In addition to [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning"), all grown from the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett")'s [genetic](/wiki/DNA "DNA") [template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template"), the GAR also had Jedi and other non-clone leadership as well as regular conscripted soldiers, though they formed the minority of soldiers in the Grand Army.

During the [waning years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") of the Republic, [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") contacted the [government](/wiki/Politics "Politics") of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") to commission the creation of a clone army, convinced that [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") would be consumed by war. As thousands of [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") joined the [Separatist movement](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") invested wartime powers in [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"). As a result, the Grand Army of the Republic was formally established, comprising thousands of clone [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") with millions more being developed in [Kaminoan](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") facilities by the start of the Clone Wars. The [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"), having served as [peacekeepers](/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency "Law enforcement agency") for a [thousand years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"), became [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") when the Senate called on the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") to lead the Grand Army against the enemies of the Republic.

For three [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"), the Grand Army fought on all fronts across a war-torn [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy"), from the [campaigns](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges") in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") to a [Separatist attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") on the Republic [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"). Through the machinations of Palpatine, [revealed](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") to the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") as the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, who was behind the war and deceiving both sides, [the clones were ultimately forced to turn against their Jedi leaders](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip"), [slaughtering](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") them throughout the galaxy and [inside](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") as directed by [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66").

After Palpatine [declared](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), the Grand Army of the Republic was absorbed by the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") and reorganized into the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Imperial_Army "Imperial Army"), allowing the remaining clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") to serve as the first generation of [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper"). However, the continued production of clone soldiers was deemed financially unfeasible, and the Empire terminated its contract with Kamino in the early months of its reign. Over time, the remaining clones in the [Imperial military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military") were decommissioned due to factors like their advanced aging and were [replaced](/wiki/Project_War-Mantle "Project War-Mantle") by [conscripted soldiers](/wiki/TK_stormtrooper "TK stormtrooper") instead.

## Description[]

### Structure[]

:   "*200,000 units are ready, with a million more well on the way.*"
:   ―Lama Su[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

 [![Clone troopers comprised the Grand Army of the Republic throughout the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/212th_Battalion.png/revision/latest?cb=20151030113059) [![Clone troopers comprised the Grand Army of the Republic throughout the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/212th_Battalion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151030113059)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/212th_Battalion.png/revision/latest?cb=20151030113059) 

Clone troopers comprised the Grand Army of the Republic throughout the Clone Wars.

 

[Clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") served as [infantry](/wiki/Infantry "Infantry") units in the Grand [Army](/wiki/Army "Army") of the [Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic").[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15) In addition to the rank-and-file [soldier](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier"), the Grand Army consisted of numerous specialists, including environment-based units like [clone cold assault troops](/wiki/Clone_cold_assault_trooper "Clone cold assault trooper") and [clone SCUBA troopers](/wiki/Clone_SCUBA_trooper "Clone SCUBA trooper"). Other variants units like [clone ordnance specialists](/wiki/Clone_ordnance_specialist "Clone ordnance specialist") and [clone trooper pilots](/wiki/Clone_trooper_pilot "Clone trooper pilot") were specially trained for specific functions, such as [bomb](/wiki/Bomb "Bomb") diffusion and flight, respectively. [ARC troopers](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando") and [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") were considered elite units in the Grand Army due to their exceptional skills and specialized training.[[16]](#cite_note-Clone_Trooper_Armor-16) Occasionally, due to accelerated aging, the Republic's clone troopers were reinforced with non-clone conscript squads.[[17]](#cite_note-Conscript_Squad-17)

The Grand Army of the Republic possessed various [military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") vehicles to support its ground forces. The principal battle [tank](/wiki/Tank "Tank") of the Grand Army was the [All Terrain Tactical Enforcer](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer"). The AT-TE's six [legs](/wiki/Limb "Limb") provided the [walker](/wiki/Walker "Walker") with increased stability, but reduced the vehicle's overall speed.[[18]](#cite_note-AT-TE-18) As mobility was a key factor in the Grand Army's effectiveness, the military was outfitted with [BARC speeders](/wiki/BARC_speeder "BARC speeder") in order to provide the [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") with increased operational range, speed, mobility, and firepower that were otherwise unavailable to foot soldiers.[[19]](#cite_note-BARC-19)

#### Unit structure[]

#### Unit Structure (Excluding Officers)[]

* **Grand Army of the Republic**—Ten [Systems Armies](/wiki/Systems_Army "Systems Army") and extra troopers (3,300,000 [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper")) led by [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Systems Army**—Two [Sector Armies](/wiki/Sector_Army "Sector Army") (294,912 troopers) led by a [High Jedi General](/wiki/High_Jedi_General "High Jedi General").[[20]](#cite_note-BMF_18-20)
* **Sector Army**[[20]](#cite_note-BMF_18-20)—Four [corps](/wiki/Corps "Corps") (147,456 troopers) led by only the most high-ranking individuals, such as the members of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Corps**—Four [legions](/wiki/Legion "Legion") (36,864 troopers) led by a [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and a [Clone Marshal Commander](/wiki/Clone_Marshal_Commander "Clone Marshal Commander").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Legion**—Four [regiments](/wiki/Regiment "Regiment") (9,216 troopers)[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8) led by a Jedi General[[21]](#cite_note-Darkness_on_Umbara-21) or a [Clone Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Regiment**—Four [battalions](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion") (2,304 troopers)[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8) led by a [Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander")[[5]](#cite_note-Rise-5) or a Clone Commander.[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Battalion**—Four [companies](/wiki/Company "Company") (576 troopers)[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8) led by a Jedi General[[22]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-22) or a Clone Commander.[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Company**—Four [platoons](/wiki/Platoon "Platoon") (144 troopers) led by a [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Platoon**—Four [squads](/wiki/Squad "Squad") (36 troopers) led by a [Clone Lieutenant](/wiki/Clone_Lieutenant "Clone Lieutenant").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Squad**—Nine troopers led by a [Clone Sergeant](/wiki/Clone_Sergeant "Clone Sergeant").[[8]](#cite_note-CL-8)
* **Brigade**—An unspecified number of troopers led by a [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") [commanding officer](/wiki/Commanding_officer "Commanding officer").[[23]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Novel-23) Two full [brigades](/wiki/Brigade "Brigade")[[24]](#cite_note-SWE_Tion_Medon-24) would be made up of multiple battalions.[[25]](#cite_note-The_End_Battalions-25) In one instance, a brigade was capable of penetrating a [world's](/wiki/Planet "Planet") orbital defenses, then taking control of an entire planet while suffering and inflicting minimal [casualties](/wiki/Death "Death").[[23]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Novel-23)

### Ranks[]

:   "*So if you're a captain, and I'm a Jedi, then technically I outrank you, right?*"  
    "*In my book,* experience *outranks everything.*"
:   ―Jedi Commander [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") and Clone Captain Rex[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26)

At first, [color](/wiki/Color "Color") was used to denote the [rank](/wiki/Military_rank "Military rank") of Grand Army clone [officers](/wiki/Officer "Officer"). This system was intended as a benefit for non-clones on the battlefield, as well as clones whose [helmet](/wiki/Armor "Armor") displays malfunctioned. It fell out of use, however, as the Jedi encouraged the clones to express their individuality. As a result, the clone army gradually adopted a new system in which they customized their [armor](/wiki/Clone_trooper_armor "Clone trooper armor") with unique color schemes and markings.[[16]](#cite_note-Clone_Trooper_Armor-16) Non-clones and non-Jedi could also serve as [Republic officers](/wiki/Republic_officer "Republic officer") in the Grand Army such as [Hodnar Borrum](/wiki/Hodnar_Borrum "Hodnar Borrum").[[27]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-27)

#### Jedi ranks[]

 [![Jedi Generals were in command of the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Heroes_of_the_Republic_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20190622223919) [![Jedi Generals were in command of the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Heroes_of_the_Republic_RotS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190622223919)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Heroes_of_the_Republic_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20190622223919) 

Jedi Generals were in command of the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

* **[High Jedi General](/wiki/High_Jedi_General "High Jedi General")**— [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") who commanded one of the ten [Systems Armies](/wiki/Systems_Army "Systems Army").[[20]](#cite_note-BMF_18-20)
* **[Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General")**—[Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") and [Jedi Masters](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master")[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26)
* **[Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander")**—Jedi [Padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), superior to clone officers and subordinate to Jedi Generals.[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26) They had authority to lead a [regiment](/wiki/Regiment "Regiment").[[5]](#cite_note-Rise-5)

### Leisure and communication[]

For leisure, the Grand Army of the Republic was supplied with a hologram-based feed identified as the [Grand Army of the Republic broadcast](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic_broadcast "Grand Army of the Republic broadcast"), which played music[[35]](#cite_note-Rookies-35) and was hosted by [Hologram VJ](/wiki/Hologram_VJ "Hologram VJ"), a [BD-3000 luxury droid](/wiki/BD-3000_luxury_droid "BD-3000 luxury droid").[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_Guide-39) Throughout the broadcast, VJ would call out specific units engaged in combat to inspire them and dedicated certain songs to those troops.[[35]](#cite_note-Rookies-35) The Grand Army was also supplied with news feeds while out on the frontline that they could listen to. One member of the GAR newsfeed was the journalist [Karama](/wiki/Karama "Karama"), who did not consider her work as actual journalism and, eventually, decided to desert from the Republic.[[40]](#cite_note-MOF-40)

## History[]

### Origins[]

:   "*Think of it. A Grand Army of the Republic. A show of strength and power like the galaxy has never seen. All stemming from you. How many men can claim such a legacy?*"
:   ―Darth Tyranus, to Jango Fett[[41]](#cite_note-Jango_Fett_1-41)

 [![The soldiers in the Grand Army of the Republic were bred in the cloning facilities of Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/Kamino_Facility.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080117183044) [![The soldiers in the Grand Army of the Republic were bred in the cloning facilities of Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/Kamino_Facility.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080117183044)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/Kamino_Facility.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080117183044) 

The soldiers in the Grand Army of the Republic were bred in the cloning facilities of Kamino.

 

The Grand Army of the Republic, shortened to the GAR,[[5]](#cite_note-Rise-5) or referred to as the Republic Army, was originally conceived by [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"), who had [foreseen](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") becoming consumed in war. Despite his removal from the ranks of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council"),[[42]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-42) whose other members rejected his ideas, Sifo-Dyas contacted the planet [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino")[[43]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-43) in [33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY "33 BBY").[[44]](#cite_note-Timelines-44) The [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan"), a [species](/wiki/Species "Species") that specialized in the science of cloning, were under the impression that Sifo-Dyas represented the interests of the council. In truth, their communication was kept secret. Unaware of this deception, the Kaminoan [cloners](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") accepted the Jedi's commission to create a clone army for the [Galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") Republic.[[43]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-43)

Returning to his Jedi duties,[[45]](#cite_note-Creationof-45) Sifo-Dyas did not live to witness the completion of his army. An unwitting pawn of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"), Sifo-Dyas was murdered by the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate")[[43]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-43) at the behest of a man named "[Tyranus](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku")"[[46]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-46)—actually the former Jedi Master Dooku, the fallen Jedi turned to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") and eventually became [apprenticed](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") to the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious").[[47]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku-47) Sifo-Dyas was unknowingly betrayed by his friend Dooku, who orchestrated his death.[[43]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-43) However, Dooku would later claim Dyas had willingly worked with him to create the clone army before the betrayal.[[46]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-46) After the death of Sifo-Dyas, the Sith secretly took over the project[[43]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-43) and selected the [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") to serve as the [genetic template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") of the clone army.[[48]](#cite_note-Jango_Fett-48)

For a time, Dooku assumed the identity of his friend in the dealings with Kamino,[[45]](#cite_note-Creationof-45) but communications between "Sifo-Dyas" and Kamino would eventually cease.[[44]](#cite_note-Timelines-44) Unaware of Sifo-Dyas's death, the Kaminoans continued with the project as the funding did not cease.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) Dooku, at some stage, also became known to the Kaminoans under his codename "Tyranus." In fact, Dooku would later allege that Sifo-Dyas had willingly helped him due to his visions.[[46]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-46)

In addition to growth acceleration and behavioral modification, an [inorganic bio-chip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") was installed into the [brain](/wiki/Brain "Brain") of every clone [trooper](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") at the early stage of their development. Sifo Dyas, who thought of the chip, intended for it to be a safeguard against rogue Jedi, but following his death, the chips were retooled by Sidious and Tyranus. The official reason behind the implant was to ensure that the clones would be more docile than their aggressive [genetic](/wiki/DNA "DNA") donor.[[49]](#cite_note-Fugitive-49) Posing as a Jedi, Tyranus presented the retooled chip to [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") and [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se"), and deceived them into believing Sifo-Dyas's intention. Unknown even to the Kaminoans,[[50]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-50) the inhibitor chips that were retooled by Sidious and Tyranus, were to ensure that the clones fulfilled their role in the [annihilation](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") in accordance with [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66").[[51]](#cite_note-Orders-51) The clones would serve as the Jedi's army,[[52]](#cite_note-Shattered-52) however, they were also an integral part in the Sith's plan for galactic domination.[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15)

### Formation[]

:   "*Do you like your army?*"  
    "*I look forward to seeing them in action.*"  
    "*They'll do their job well. I'll guarantee that.*"
:   ―Jango Fett and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

As a result of the clone troopers' accelerated growth, the first two hundred thousand soldiers were completed within a decade[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)—approximately ten [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the Battle of Naboo[[53]](#cite_note-ten_years-53) and [twenty-two years](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY") before the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin").[[12]](#cite_note-Founded_date-12) By then the galaxy stood on the brink of war,[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) as predicted by Sifo-Dyas,[[43]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-43) due to a group of secessionist [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") and powerful corporations. Seeking independence from the Galactic Republic, they combined their resources to form the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"),[[54]](#cite_note-CIS-54) an act which the Republic refused to recognize.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

 [![Within ten years of their creation, the first clone trooper battalions were ready to serve the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic.png/revision/latest?cb=20210619204924) [![Within ten years of their creation, the first clone trooper battalions were ready to serve the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20210619204924)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic.png/revision/latest?cb=20210619204924) 

Within ten years of their creation, the first clone trooper battalions were ready to serve the Galactic Republic.

 

Vowing to preserve the unity of the thousand-year Republic, [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") Sheev Palpatine attempted to negotiate the Separatists' return to the Republic with the aid of the [Loyalist Committee](/wiki/Loyalist_Committee "Loyalist Committee") and the Jedi Council. Around the same time, the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") was divided in their response to the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"). Some [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") advocated for the passage of the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"), which would enable the Republic to organize a military force to defend it. Other senators such as [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") opposed the bill under the belief that it would provoke a full-scale war between the Republic and the Separatists.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

The matter was ultimately settled when the [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") discovered both the Kamino-produced clone army and the largest army of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") that the Separatists constructed on the planet [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"). Convinced that the senators would never authorize the creation of a military on their own before the Separatists attacked the Republic, [Junior Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") called on the Senate to empower the Supreme Chancellor with the authority to end the crisis of the Separatist movement[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) through the [Emergency Powers Act](/wiki/Emergency_Powers_Act "Emergency Powers Act").[[55]](#cite_note-Jar_Jar_card-55) Scared of the Separatists attacking with their battle droids,[[56]](#cite_note-Palpatine_biography_gallery_Image_10-56) the Senate enthusiastically supported Binks' proposal; accordingly Palpatine accepted the mandate and announced the formation of the Grand Army of the Republic.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

### Clone Wars[]

#### Across the frontlines[]

:   "*What's the point of all this? I mean, why?*"  
    "*I don't know, sir. I don't think anybody knows. But I* do *know that someday this war is gonna end.*"  
    "*Then what? We're soldiers. What happens to us then?*"
:   ―Rex and [Fives](/wiki/Fives "Fives") following the Umbara Campaign[[37]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-37)

 [![At the time of its introduction, the Grand Army of the Republic represented the future of galactic warfare.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160125191812) [![At the time of its introduction, the Grand Army of the Republic represented the future of galactic warfare.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20160125191812)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160125191812) 

At the time of its introduction, the Grand Army of the Republic represented the future of galactic warfare.

 

After a decade of development and training, the first generation of clone troopers was called into action. Placed under the leadership of [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), the Grand Army of the Republic made its debut in the [Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), engaging the [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") army with the element of surprise on their side. Clone troopers fought side by side as they repelled the Battle droids from the battlefield, ultimately annihilating the entire droid army, the Grand Army claimed victory in the greatest battle of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars")—so-named for the clones who composed the Republic's armed forces.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

Throughout the conflict, the Grand Army of the Republic was deployed across the galaxy in order to put an end to the rebellion of the Separatists. The Jedi Knights assumed direct command over the clone troopers, becoming [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") of the Grand Army. As the Clone Wars progressed, more clone troopers sacrificed their lives out of loyalty to the Jedi and the Supreme Chancellor.[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15) While the clones had been engineered to serve as soldiers in the Grand Army, they were also encouraged by the Jedi to develop their own distinct identities, consequently resulting in a wave of greater individuality and creative-thinking that spread through the clone ranks. As such, special unit markings and color patterns became increasingly common within the Grand Army.[[16]](#cite_note-Clone_Trooper_Armor-16)

 [![Over three years, the Grand Army clashed with the Separatist Droid Army during the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Hasbro-ClonevB1.png/revision/latest?cb=20240426024922) [![Over three years, the Grand Army clashed with the Separatist Droid Army during the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Hasbro-ClonevB1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20240426024922)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Hasbro-ClonevB1.png/revision/latest?cb=20240426024922) 

Over three years, the Grand Army clashed with the Separatist Droid Army during the Clone Wars.

 

The Grand Army of the Republic fought on all fronts for three years[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15) while Palpatine shut down efforts at diplomacy,[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) claiming the victory of the GAR was the only chance the galaxy had at peace[[10]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-10) and that the Separatists had rejected every offer of peace the Republic outstretched.[[57]](#cite_note-Heroes-57) One particular soldier—[Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex")[[58]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars_Episode_Guide_5-58) of the elite [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion")[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59)—became a legend amongst the troops, becoming considered the hero of the Grand Army.[[58]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars_Episode_Guide_5-58) While clone troopers formed the backbone of the Republic's military might,[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15) non-clone servicepeople, such as the [Wookiee warriors](/wiki/Wookiee_warrior "Wookiee warrior") of the planet [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk")[[60]](#cite_note-Rebels_VG-60) and the [military defense forces](/wiki/Roon%27s_military_defense_forces "Roon's military defense forces") of [Roon](/wiki/Roon "Roon"), also fought for the Republic during the conflict. In fact, a full company of those [Roonian](/wiki/Roonian "Roonian") soldiers were absorbed into the ranks of the Grand Army's [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") for the [Battle of Abrion Bridge](/wiki/Battle_of_Abrion_Bridge "Battle of Abrion Bridge"), where Jedi General [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), Clone Commander [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody"), and Roonian Commander [Mekedrix](/wiki/Mekedrix "Mekedrix") led a combined force of clone troopers and Roonians in a bloody battle.[[61]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_3-61)

Another non-clone member of the Grand Army was an explosives expert named [Skelly](/wiki/Skelly "Skelly"), who was the lone Republic soldier to walk away from the [Battle of Slag's Pit](/wiki/Battle_of_Slag%27s_Pit "Battle of Slag's Pit").[[62]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-62) Additionally, an individual named [Sefin Garoby](/wiki/Sefin_Garoby "Sefin Garoby") worked with the Grand Army during the war and traveled with a contingent of clone troopers to the planet [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), only to crash on the obscure moon [Toshara](/wiki/Toshara "Toshara") along the way. With all clones dying in the crash, the native [Tosharans](/wiki/Tosharan "Tosharan") helped Garoby organize a funeral for the [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") and helped Garoby repair their transport starship, ensuring the mission could continue. Garoby was awed by the compassion of the Tosharans and left behind a [protocol droid](/wiki/Sefin_Garoby%27s_protocol_droid "Sefin Garoby's protocol droid") so they could prepare for contact with the wider galaxy.[[63]](#cite_note-Outlaws-63)

#### Execute Order 66[]

:   "*How widespread is this?*"  
    "*Ahsoka, it's all of us. The entire Grand Army of the Republic has been ordered to hunt down and destroy the Jedi Knights.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano and Rex — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/HowWidespread-Shattered.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250327205815)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:HowWidespread-Shattered.flac "File:HowWidespread-Shattered.flac"))[[52]](#cite_note-Shattered-52)

As the end of the war drew near, clone troopers continued to see action from [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") to [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk")[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15) and [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"). Following the deaths of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Tyranus, which was orchestrated by Sidious when he betrayed and caused the death of his apprentice in the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"), and [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") in the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau"), the Separatists were all but defeated. However, by then the Jedi Council discovered the Supreme Chancellor's true identity—Sheev Palpatine and Darth Sidious were one and the same; the leader of the Galactic Senate was the enigmatic Sith Lord who secretly instigated the war and controlled both sides in the war, as well as was deceiving both sides.[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3)

 [![The Grand Army turned against the Jedi Order after receiving Order 66 from the Supreme Chancellor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/Depa-troopers-Order-66.png/revision/latest?cb=20211231053511) [![The Grand Army turned against the Jedi Order after receiving Order 66 from the Supreme Chancellor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/Depa-troopers-Order-66.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20211231053511)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/Depa-troopers-Order-66.png/revision/latest?cb=20211231053511) 

The Grand Army turned against the Jedi Order after receiving Order 66 from the Supreme Chancellor.

 

Realizing they had been deceived, several masters on the council moved swiftly to arrest the Chancellor before he could destroy the Jedi Order and the Republic, but their efforts ultimately ended in failure. Using this [incident](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") to frame the Jedi Order for treason, Sidious declared that all Jedi were now enemies of the state.[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) It was then that the Sith unleashed their secret weapon—the Grand Army of the Republic. Sidious broadcasted Order 66 to the clone troopers who were spread throughout the galaxy. The order activated the clones' secret programming as a result of the inhibitor chips in their brains, conditioning the clones to believe that the Jedi were traitors to the Republic that needed to be executed.[[52]](#cite_note-Shattered-52)

The clones complied with Order 66 without question, turning their weapons on the Jedi and executing them across numerous worlds. At the same time, the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on Coruscant was attacked by the 501st Legion led by the former Jedi Knight [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), who had betrayed the Jedi and joined the Sith as Sidious' new apprentice, Darth Vader.[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) The Jedi were caught off guard by their Troopers betrayal, but only a handful survived. With the the Jedi Order virtually destroyed and the Grand Army under the Chancellor's control,[[64]](#cite_note-Aftermath-64) Sidious proclaimed himself [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the newly established [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire").[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) Ultimately, the Grand Army of the Republic was an asset that enabled Sidious to establish a Sith dictatorship over the galaxy.[[15]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-15)

### Legacy[]

#### A new era[]

:   "*You and your kind brought peace to the galaxy. Why would you lower yourself to fight with traitors? Where is your loyalty?*"  
    "*My loyalty was to the Republic, not your Empire.*"  
    "*I serve the order* you *put into place, Captain.*"
:   ―[Brom Titus](/wiki/Brom_Titus "Brom Titus") and Rex[[65]](#cite_note-Stealth_Strike-65)

 [![The early Imperial Army consisted of clone troopers who once fought for the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Clone-stormtroopers-Raxus.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111211411) [![The early Imperial Army consisted of clone troopers who once fought for the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Clone-stormtroopers-Raxus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220111211411)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Clone-stormtroopers-Raxus.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111211411) 

The early Imperial Army consisted of clone troopers who once fought for the Galactic Republic.

 

As the formation of the Empire marked the end of the Galactic Republic, the Grand Army of the Republic became the basis of the [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military")—the armed forces of the Emperor's [new government](/wiki/New_Order "New Order").[[66]](#cite_note-Tarkin-66) Accordingly, the Republic clone troopers transitioned into [Imperial stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper").[[67]](#cite_note-Stormtroopers-67) With vast portions of the galaxy unconquered, the Empire embarked on a massive militarization program to eliminate the remaining [Separatist holdouts](/wiki/Separatist_holdouts "Separatist holdouts"), enforce the Emperor's authority, and expand the Empire's growing dominion.[[66]](#cite_note-Tarkin-66)

With the end of the Clone Wars, however, high ranking Imperials such as [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") questioned the continued usage of the clones. The production of clone troopers was a "cost prohibitive" enterprise according to Tarkin, who believed that order could be maintained by a less expensive force of [conscripted soldiers](/wiki/Project_War-Mantle "Project War-Mantle").[[64]](#cite_note-Aftermath-64) Furthermore, Tarkin was concerned by the individuality clones had developed under Jedi leadership that allowed them to question orders.[[68]](#cite_note-The_Summit-68) Another issue was that the clones had been created for the Republic, not the new empire that recruits would swear themselves to.[[69]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-69)

 [![Human conscripts supplanted genetically engineered soldiers in the Empire's stormtrooper ranks.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Stormtroopers-TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20210704000211) [![Human conscripts supplanted genetically engineered soldiers in the Empire's stormtrooper ranks.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Stormtroopers-TCW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20210704000211)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Stormtroopers-TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20210704000211) 

Human conscripts supplanted genetically engineered soldiers in the Empire's stormtrooper ranks.

 

Notably, the clones' skills deteriorated with the accelerated speed of their aging process, further leading the Empire to prefer human recruits and conscripts over cloned soldiers.[[67]](#cite_note-Stormtroopers-67) Overtime, clones were removed from combat duty and instead given the task of managing various Imperial projects. By this time, many clones felt bitter and horrified at their actions during Order 66, even though it was out of their control.[[70]](#cite_note-70) Clone [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") Rex went on to join the [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell") of the early rebel movement during the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War").[[71]](#cite_note-The_Lost_Commanders-71)

#### Last march of the GAR[]

:   "*One last glorious day in the Grand Army of the Republic.*"
:   ―Captain Rex[[72]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-72)

During a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Agamar_(2_BBY) "Mission to Agamar (2 BBY)") to retrieve munitions from a crashed [Separatist supply ship](/wiki/Unidentified_DH-Omni_Support_Vessel_(Agamar) "Unidentified DH-Omni Support Vessel (Agamar)") on[[72]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-72) the planet[[73]](#cite_note-Last_Battle_Guide-73) of [Agamar](/wiki/Agamar "Agamar"), however, Rex and his allies, two of which were the Jedi Knight [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") and his Padawan, [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), found a surviving [Separatist holdout](/wiki/Agamar_garrison "Agamar garrison") commanded by a [ST-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid](/wiki/ST-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "ST-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") named General [Kalani](/wiki/Kalani "Kalani"). Taking another member of their team, [Garazeb Orrelios](/wiki/Garazeb_Orrelios "Garazeb Orrelios"), captive, Kalani forced the Clone Captain and Jedi to fight a final battle of the Clone Wars to finally prove which faction was superior. Rex found himself determined to win the contest against his old enemies, but Bridger stopped the Clone Captain from killing Kalani when they reached the command center, having realized the clones, Jedi, and battle droids had all lost the war. The Padawan questioned who truly had won the conflict, and Orrelios then pointed out that the Empire had and that an Imperial force was arriving on Agamar. Though Rex was initially reluctant to join with the battle droids, Bridger convinced Kalani to fight the Empire alongside them.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-72)

 [![Ezra Bridger surmised that both the Grand Army of the Republic and the Separatist Droid Army lost the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Ezra_reasoning_with_Rex_and_Kalani.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161107074028) [![Ezra Bridger surmised that both the Grand Army of the Republic and the Separatist Droid Army lost the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Ezra_reasoning_with_Rex_and_Kalani.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161107074028)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Ezra_reasoning_with_Rex_and_Kalani.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161107074028) 

Ezra Bridger surmised that both the Grand Army of the Republic and the Separatist Droid Army lost the Clone Wars.

 

Rex did agree to join with the Separatists. Thus, the rebels and droids planned to delay the Empire's advance, giving them a chance to escape aboard [*Sheathipede*-class transport shuttles](/wiki/Sheathipede-class_transport_shuttle "Sheathipede-class transport shuttle"). Once the rebels and droids stationed themselves in the [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar"), Rex remarked that he was serving one last [day](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") in the Grand Army, and, after Kalani noted that he had never attempted such a desperate plan, Rex joked that it was the reason the Republic Military had always won. Kalani rebutted this, noting that there had been Republic loses during the conflict, before their combined forces engaged the Imperial walkers and stormtroopers. To take out one of the [All Terrain Armored Transports](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Transport_(Prototype) "All Terrain Armored Transport (Prototype)"), Bridger and Jarrus deflected blaster bolts into [proton bombs](/wiki/Proton_bomb "Proton bomb"), giving the rebels and droids their chance to flee. Though one of the battle droids' [shuttles](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle") was taken out, the rebel's [*Sheathipede* shuttle](/wiki/Phantom_II "Phantom II") and the one containing Kalani and several [B1 battle droids](/wiki/B1-series_battle_droid "B1-series battle droid") escaped the planet. Once off-world, both factions spoke via a [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram"), and Rex and Kalani both agreed they had now all won the Clone Wars. Satisfied that the conflict was over, Kalani and his droids parted ways with the rebels, believing they would likely lose the war against the Empire.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-72)

#### Continued legacy[]

Few clones continued to serve in the stormtrooper ranks by the time after the Battle of Yavin; [ISB](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Alecia Beck](/wiki/Alecia_Beck "Alecia Beck") believed [Sergeant](/wiki/Sergeant "Sergeant") [Torrent](/wiki/Torrent "Torrent") to be one of the last Kamino-produced clones who were still in service to the Imperial Military.[[74]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-74) During the time of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"), the Grand Army was still referenced in military circles, with [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") belittling [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux")'s [troops](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper"), suggesting a clone army would be a stronger force.[[75]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-75)

## Groups[]

### Armies and corps[]

:   "*It won't be long before the armies of the Republic track us here.*"
:   ―Grievous, to the [Executive Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council")[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3)

 [![The Grand Army of the Republic was arranged in various formations.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/ImperialMarch-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20210903040636) [![The Grand Army of the Republic was arranged in various formations.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/ImperialMarch-AOTC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210903040636)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/ImperialMarch-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20210903040636) 

The Grand Army of the Republic was arranged in various formations.

 

The Grand Army of the Republic was composed of ten [Systems Armies](/wiki/Systems_Army "Systems Army") that each contained two [Sector Armies](/wiki/Sector_Army "Sector Army").[[20]](#cite_note-BMF_18-20) One such Systems Army was the [Third Systems Army](/wiki/Third_Systems_Army "Third Systems Army").[[76]](#cite_note-Kenobi-76) The first six Sector Armies were reserve commands, the next six were northern quadrant, and the remaining eight were southern quadrant units. Sector Armies included the [1st Sector Army](/wiki/1st_Sector_Army "1st Sector Army"), the [4th Sector Army](/wiki/4th_Sector_Army "4th Sector Army"), the [6th Sector Army](/wiki/6th_Sector_Army "6th Sector Army"), the [7th Sector Army](/wiki/7th_Sector_Army "7th Sector Army"), the [8th Sector Army](/wiki/8th_Sector_Army "8th Sector Army"), and the [12th Sector Army](/wiki/12th_Sector_Army "12th Sector Army").[[20]](#cite_note-BMF_18-20)

Subsequently, the GAR consisted of many corps, which included the [7th Sky Corps](/wiki/7th_Sky_Corps "7th Sky Corps") of Jedi General [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") and Clone Marshal Commander [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody"),[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) the [flame trooper corps](/wiki/Flame_trooper_corps "Flame trooper corps"),[[5]](#cite_note-Rise-5) the [9th Assault Corps](/wiki/9th_Assault_Corps "9th Assault Corps"),[[77]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_and_Other_Force_Users-77) the [21st Nova Corps](/wiki/Galactic_Marines "Galactic Marines") under Jedi General Ki-Adi-Mundi and Clone Marshal Commander [Bacara](/wiki/Bacara "Bacara"), the 41st Elite Corps under Jedi General [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli") and Clone Commander [Gree](/wiki/Gree_(clone_trooper) "Gree (clone trooper)"),[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) the [87th Sentinel Corps](/wiki/87th_Sentinel_Corps "87th Sentinel Corps") which specialized in urban warfare,[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) the [91st Mobile Reconnaissance Corps](/wiki/91st_Mobile_Reconnaissance_Corps "91st Mobile Reconnaissance Corps") under Jedi Generals [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia "Adi Gallia"), and [Stass Allie](/wiki/Stass_Allie "Stass Allie") alongside Clone Commander [Neyo](/wiki/Neyo "Neyo"), and the [327th Star Corps](/wiki/327th_Star_Corps "327th Star Corps") under Jedi General [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura") and Clone Commander [Bly](/wiki/Bly "Bly").[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) The 9th Assault Corps was large enough that another corps, the 41st, could be organized under it.[[77]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_and_Other_Force_Users-77) Clone medics, even if they were assigned to detachments such as legions, were additionally organized under the [Republic Medic Corps](/wiki/Republic_Medic_Corps "Republic Medic Corps").[[78]](#cite_note-Join_the_Battle-78)

### Legions and divisions[]

:   "*I'll divide the 501st, make a new division under Ahsoka's command.*"  
    "*Unfortunately, Ahsoka is no longer a part of the Grand Army of the Republic.*"  
    "*We'll promote Rex to Commander and have him lead the new division. Ahsoka can go with him as an advisor.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/RexPromotion-OFNF.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250327205915)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:RexPromotion-OFNF.flac "File:RexPromotion-OFNF.flac"))[[79]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-79)

 [![The 501st Legion served under Jedi General Anakin Skywalker throughout the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Knightfall2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208032337) [![The 501st Legion served under Jedi General Anakin Skywalker throughout the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Knightfall2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130208032337)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Knightfall2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208032337) 

The 501st Legion served under Jedi General Anakin Skywalker throughout the Clone Wars.

 

Additionally, legions within the GAR included the [481st Legion](/wiki/481st_Legion "481st Legion"),[[80]](#cite_note-Nexus-80) the [Third Legion](/wiki/Third_Legion "Third Legion"),[[81]](#cite_note-Assassin-81) and the famed [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion"),[[82]](#cite_note-HC_16-82) an elite detachment that served Jedi General [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and Jedi Commander Ahsoka Tano alongside Clone Captain,[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) later Commander, Rex,[[83]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-83) with [Appo](/wiki/Appo "Appo") also arising to the rank of Clone Commander in time.[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) The elite [187th Legion](/wiki/187th_Legion "187th Legion") was led by Master Windu.[[84]](#cite_note-Tank_Reveal-84)

Divisions varied in size, and could be organized under legions[[79]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-79) or even small-level formations such as [battalions](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion"). Divisions included the [181st Armor Division](/wiki/181st_Armor_Division "181st Armor Division"),[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) the [224th Clone Division](/wiki/224th_Imperial_Armored_Division "224th Imperial Armored Division"),[[85]](#cite_note-TOG-85) and the [332nd Division](/wiki/332nd_Division "332nd Division") of the 501st Legion.[[79]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-79)

### Brigades, regiments, and battalions[]

:   "*Remember, General Krell, the entire invasion depends on your battalion.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to [Pong Krell](/wiki/Pong_Krell "Pong Krell")[[86]](#cite_note-The_General-86)

 [![The 212th was a battalion in the Grand Army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/TCW_Waxer_platoon_stops_firing.png/revision/latest?cb=20180722034114) [![The 212th was a battalion in the Grand Army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/TCW_Waxer_platoon_stops_firing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180722034114)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/TCW_Waxer_platoon_stops_firing.png/revision/latest?cb=20180722034114) 

The 212th was a battalion in the Grand Army.

 

A [brigade](/wiki/Brigade "Brigade") within the GAR included the [Special Operations Brigade](/wiki/Special_Operations_Brigade "Special Operations Brigade"), which was the [special forces](/wiki/Special_forces "Special forces") branch of the Grand Army of the Republic.[[6]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_21-6) A [tank brigade](/wiki/Unidentified_tank_brigade "Unidentified tank brigade") served in the 501st.[[87]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-87) Further down the hierarchy of military formations were regiments, which included a [regiment](/wiki/Tacks%27s_regiment "Tacks's regiment") led by Clone Commander [Tacks](/wiki/Tacks "Tacks"), a [regiment](/wiki/Yoda%27s_regiment "Yoda's regiment") which served in the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"),[[88]](#cite_note-Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel-88) and a [scout regiment](/wiki/Unidentified_Galactic_Republic_regiment "Unidentified Galactic Republic regiment") that was dispatched to the Wild Space planet [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth").[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26)

Battalions in the GAR included the [302nd Battalion](/wiki/302nd_Battalion "302nd Battalion"), which was staffed by Commander [Theo](/wiki/Theo_(clone_trooper) "Theo (clone trooper)"), Captain [Sparks](/wiki/Sparks_(clone_trooper) "Sparks (clone trooper)"), and Captain [Raptor](/wiki/Raptor "Raptor"),[[89]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-89) the [9th Engineering Battalion](/wiki/9th_Engineering_Battalion "9th Engineering Battalion"),[[90]](#cite_note-Friends_Like_These-90) the [13th Battalion](/wiki/13th_Battalion "13th Battalion")[[91]](#cite_note-Art_of_JFO-91) which was led by Jedi General [Jaro Tapal](/wiki/Jaro_Tapal "Jaro Tapal") and a [Clone Commander](/wiki/Unidentified_Clone_Commander_(13th_Battalion) "Unidentified Clone Commander (13th Battalion)"),[[92]](#cite_note-Jedi_Fallen_Order-92) the [41st Scout Battalion](/wiki/41st_Scout_Battalion "41st Scout Battalion") led by Jedi General [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") and part of the 41st Elite Corps,[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) the [104th Battalion](/wiki/104th_Battalion "104th Battalion") under the command of Jedi General [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon") and Clone Commander [Wolffe](/wiki/Wolffe "Wolffe"),[[22]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-22) the [187th Battalion](/wiki/187th_Battalion "187th Battalion") led by General Windu,[[93]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-93) the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") under Marshal Commander Cody and within the 7th Sky Corps,[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) the [442nd Siege Battalion](/wiki/442nd_Siege_Battalion "442nd Siege Battalion"),[[94]](#cite_note-Hasbro-94) the [Carnivore Battalion](/wiki/Carnivore_Battalion "Carnivore Battalion") within the 501st,[[95]](#cite_note-Cargo-95) the [battalion](/wiki/Jet%27s_battalion "Jet's battalion") led by General Ki-Adi-Mundi and Clone Commander [Jet](/wiki/Jet "Jet"),[[96]](#cite_note-Ki-Adi-Mundi-96) a [battalion](/wiki/Depa_Billaba%27s_battalion "Depa Billaba's battalion") commanded by Jedi General [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba") and Clone Commander [Grey](/wiki/Grey_(clone_trooper) "Grey (clone trooper)") as well as a [subsequent battalion](/wiki/Depa_Billaba%27s_second_battalion "Depa Billaba's second battalion") after the first was destroyed,[[97]](#cite_note-Kanan_7-97) the 501st's [Execute Battalion](/wiki/Execute_Battalion "Execute Battalion"),[[95]](#cite_note-Cargo-95) the [One-Eighty-Fourth Attack
