[Blitz](/wiki/Blitz "Blitz"), [Colt](/wiki/Colt "Colt"), and [Havoc](/wiki/Havoc_(ARC_trooper) "Havoc (ARC trooper)").[[29]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-29)

### Garrisons, squadrons, companies, smaller divisions, and batteries[]

:   "*Green Company, prepare to repel the enemy.*"
:   ―Gree[[99]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-99)

A [garrison](/wiki/Garrison "Garrison") within the GAR was the [Outer Rim garrison](/wiki/Outer_Rim_garrison "Outer Rim garrison") led by Jedi General [Ima-Gun Di](/wiki/Ima-Gun_Di "Ima-Gun Di") and Clone Captain [Keeli](/wiki/Keeli "Keeli").[[100]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-100) Additionally, [squadrons](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") in the Grand Army were a [SPHA-T squadron](/wiki/Unidentified_SPHA-T_squadron "Unidentified SPHA-T squadron") that served on Geonosis,[[101]](#cite_note-SW_Encyclopedia-101) the [Lightning Squadron](/wiki/Lightning_Squadron "Lightning Squadron") under the command of Clone Commander [Ponds](/wiki/Ponds "Ponds"),[[102]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-102) Anakin Skywalker's [Bravo Squadron](/wiki/Bravo_Squadron_(Galactic_Republic) "Bravo Squadron (Galactic Republic)"),[[103]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-103) and a [tank squadron](/wiki/Unidentified_tank_squadron "Unidentified tank squadron") that participated on [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia").[[32]](#cite_note-Padawan_Lost-32) A [battery](/wiki/Unidentified_tank_battery "Unidentified tank battery") of [tanks](/wiki/Tank "Tank") served in the army as well.[[87]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-87)

 [![Torrent Company was a sub-unit of the 501st Legion that fought on Christophsis and Teth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Captain_Rex_and_his_clone_troopers_on_Teth.png/revision/latest?cb=20180830194405) [![Torrent Company was a sub-unit of the 501st Legion that fought on Christophsis and Teth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Captain_Rex_and_his_clone_troopers_on_Teth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180830194405)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Captain_Rex_and_his_clone_troopers_on_Teth.png/revision/latest?cb=20180830194405) 

Torrent Company was a sub-unit of the 501st Legion that fought on Christophsis and Teth.

 

Companies within the ground forces of the Republic were [Sivad's company](/wiki/Sivad%27s_company "Sivad's company"),[[34]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-34) the [332nd Company](/wiki/332nd_Company "332nd Company")[[104]](#cite_note-9_Best_Helmets-104) within the 501st Legion,[[83]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-83) [Ghost Company](/wiki/Ghost_Company "Ghost Company") of the 7th Sky Corps,[[105]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-105) [Green Company](/wiki/Green_Company "Green Company") of the 41st Elite Corps and led by [Green Leader](/wiki/Green_Leader_(clone_trooper) "Green Leader (clone trooper)"),[[99]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-99) a [company](/wiki/Monnk%27s_company "Monnk's company") under Clone Commander [Monnk](/wiki/Monnk "Monnk"),[[106]](#cite_note-Water_War-106) a [company](/wiki/Aayla_Secura%27s_company "Aayla Secura's company") of the 327th Star Corps,[[107]](#cite_note-Destiny-107) a [company](/wiki/Tualon_Yaluna%27s_company "Tualon Yaluna's company") under Jedi General [Josk Nivar](/wiki/Josk_Nivar "Josk Nivar") and then Jedi General [Tualon Yaluna](/wiki/Tualon_Yaluna "Tualon Yaluna"),[[108]](#cite_note-Inquisitor-108) [Red Company](/wiki/Red_Company "Red Company") of the 41st Elite Corps,[[109]](#cite_note-HC_60_scout-109) [Tango Company](/wiki/Tango_Company "Tango Company") led by Clone Lieutenant [Trap](/wiki/Trap "Trap"),[[110]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-110) and [Torrent Company](/wiki/Torrent_Company "Torrent Company") that was under the 501st Legion.[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26) The [212th Recon Division](/wiki/212th_Recon_Division "212th Recon Division"), overall led by Cody, was part of the 212th Attack Battalion.[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59)

### Platoons, squads, and training units[]

:   "*I left my squad when they needed me. I was scared. I was…* wrong*.*"
:   ―Charlie[[111]](#cite_note-Battle_Tales_4-111)

Platoons within the GAR included the [41st Ranger Platoon](/wiki/41st_Ranger_Platoon "41st Ranger Platoon") within the 41st Elite Corps,[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) a [platoon](/wiki/Rex%27s_platoon "Rex's platoon") led by Rex of the 501st Legion,[[21]](#cite_note-Darkness_on_Umbara-21) a [platoon](/wiki/Unidentified_platoon_(Galactic_Republic) "Unidentified platoon (Galactic Republic)") with cold-weather gear also within the 501st,[[112]](#cite_note-Trespass-112) and a [platoon](/wiki/Waxer%27s_platoon "Waxer's platoon") led by [Platoon leader](/wiki/Platoon_leader "Platoon leader") [Waxer](/wiki/Waxer "Waxer") from the 7th Sky Corps.[[37]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-37)

 [![Delta Squad was a team of elite clone commandos trained for special operations.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/DeltaSquad-WOTM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130524024028) [![Delta Squad was a team of elite clone commandos trained for special operations.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/DeltaSquad-WOTM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130524024028)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/DeltaSquad-WOTM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130524024028) 

Delta Squad was a team of elite clone commandos trained for special operations.

 

Squads within the Grand Army were a [squad](/wiki/Charlie%27s_squad "Charlie's squad") what included the [trooper](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") [Charlie](/wiki/Charlie "Charlie"),[[111]](#cite_note-Battle_Tales_4-111) a [squad](/wiki/Fil%27s_Squad "Fil's Squad") led by Clone Commander [Fil](/wiki/Fil "Fil"),[[113]](#cite_note-Lair-113) [First squad](/wiki/First_squad "First squad") from the 501st Legion,[[112]](#cite_note-Trespass-112) an over strength [501st squad](/wiki/Rex%27s_squad "Rex's squad") under the command of Rex,[[114]](#cite_note-Plan-114) the [Wolfpack](/wiki/Wolfpack "Wolfpack") squad of the 104th,[[34]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-34) a [squad](/wiki/Heater%27s_squad "Heater's squad") led by the trooper [Heater](/wiki/Heater_(clone_trooper) "Heater (clone trooper)"),[[111]](#cite_note-Battle_Tales_4-111) a [squad](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi%27s_squad "Ki-Adi-Mundi's squad") led by General Ki-Adi-Mundi within the 21st Nova Corps,[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) a [droid squadron](/wiki/R2-D2%27s_battle_droid_squadron "R2-D2's battle droid squadron") under orders from [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"),[[115]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-115) [Rostu Squad](/wiki/Rostu_Squad "Rostu Squad") from Depa Billaba's second battalion,[[116]](#cite_note-K2-116) a [squad](/wiki/Skywalker%27s_squad "Skywalker's squad") led by Jedi General Anakin Skywalker from the 501st.[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26) During the First Battle of Geonosis, Yoda led a [squad](/wiki/Yoda%27s_squad "Yoda's squad") within his larger regiment[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) before commanding a [small squad](/wiki/Yoda%27s_squad_(Rugosa) "Yoda's squad (Rugosa)")[[117]](#cite_note-TCW_Official_Collector's_Edition-117) from the [diplomatic service](/wiki/Diplomatic_service "Diplomatic service") on [Rugosa](/wiki/Rugosa "Rugosa").[[118]](#cite_note-Ambush-118)

Training units included the [322nd](/wiki/322nd "322nd"),[[119]](#cite_note-Death_Trap-119) [Bravo Squad](/wiki/Bravo_Squad_(clone_cadets) "Bravo Squad (clone cadets)"),[[29]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-29) the [Clone Youth Brigade](/wiki/Clone_Youth_Brigade "Clone Youth Brigade"),[[119]](#cite_note-Death_Trap-119) and [Domino Squad](/wiki/Domino_Squad "Domino Squad").[[29]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-29)

### Other units[]

:   "*This next one goes out to the Mud Jumpers of the 224th, slugging it out on Mimban. Keep your heads down and your seals tight, boys.*"
:   ―Hologram VJ — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Mudjumpers.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329115631)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Mudjumpers.flac "File:Mudjumpers.flac"))[[35]](#cite_note-Rookies-35)

 [![Military security on the Republic capital was provided by the clone shock troopers of the Coruscant Guard.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/CoruscantGuardssearching.png/revision/latest?cb=20200606004751) [![Military security on the Republic capital was provided by the clone shock troopers of the Coruscant Guard.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/CoruscantGuardssearching.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200606004751)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/CoruscantGuardssearching.png/revision/latest?cb=20200606004751) 

Military security on the Republic capital was provided by the clone shock troopers of the Coruscant Guard.

 

There were other units of varying formation size that were also part of the Grand Army of the Republic. These units included the [Calm Tree](/wiki/Calm_Tree "Calm Tree"), [Snow Wolves](/wiki/Snow_Wolves "Snow Wolves"), and [Wildfire](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") teams of the 501st.[[120]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus_EG-120) Another unit was the [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard")[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) and its diplomatic service subunit.[[121]](#cite_note-Concept_Art_Gallery-121) Alongside the planet's [garrison](/wiki/Kamino_garrison "Kamino garrison"),[[87]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-87) a [security force](/wiki/Kamino_security "Kamino security") on Kamino was led by Jedi General [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti") and a [Clone Captain](/wiki/Unidentified_Clone_Captain_(Kamino) "Unidentified Clone Captain (Kamino)").[[49]](#cite_note-Fugitive-49)

Other units included a [unit](/wiki/Chiata%27s_unit "Chiata's unit") led by Jedi General [Chiata](/wiki/Chiata "Chiata") and a [Clone Commander](/wiki/Unidentified_Clone_Commander_(Zeffo) "Unidentified Clone Commander (Zeffo)"),[[92]](#cite_note-Jedi_Fallen_Order-92) the [unit](/wiki/Doom%27s_unit "Doom's unit") led by Jedi Generals [Tiplee](/wiki/Tiplee "Tiplee") and [Tiplar](/wiki/Tiplar "Tiplar") alongside Clone Commander [Doom](/wiki/Doom "Doom"),[[122]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-122) a [unit](/wiki/Halsey%27s_unit "Halsey's unit") led by Jedi General [Halsey](/wiki/Halsey "Halsey") and Clone Commander [Trauma](/wiki/Trauma "Trauma"),[[123]](#cite_note-Monster-123) a [unit](/wiki/Leh%27ahnyo_Vas%27_unit "Leh'ahnyo Vas' unit") that was commanded by [Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") [Leh'ahnyo Vas](/wiki/Leh%27ahnyo_Vas "Leh'ahnyo Vas") and their [master](/wiki/Leh%27ahnyo_Vas%27_master "Leh'ahnyo Vas' master"),[[5]](#cite_note-Rise-5) a [unit](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos%27s_unit "Quinlan Vos's unit") led by General [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos"),[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) the [Mud Jumpers](/wiki/Mud_Jumpers "Mud Jumpers") from the 224th Division,[[85]](#cite_note-TOG-85) a [clone security force](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia_clone_security_force "Orto Plutonia clone security force") on [Orto Plutonia](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia "Orto Plutonia"),[[112]](#cite_note-Trespass-112) a [unit](/wiki/Rishi_Station_unit "Rishi Station unit") that protected the [Rishi Station](/wiki/Rishi_Station "Rishi Station"),[[35]](#cite_note-Rookies-35) a [military team](/wiki/Skywalker%27s_team "Skywalker's team") within the 501st,[[124]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-124) and a [squad](/wiki/Slick%27s_squad "Slick's squad") of the Grand Army led by Clone Sergeant [Slick](/wiki/Slick "Slick").[[125]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-125)

## Vehicles and machinery[]

:   "*We need more firepower! Send in the walkers!*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker[[30]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-30)

 [![The All Terrain Tactical Enforcer was the main battle tank of the GAR.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Battle_of_Malastare.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911231558) [![The All Terrain Tactical Enforcer was the main battle tank of the GAR.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Battle_of_Malastare.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120911231558)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Battle_of_Malastare.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911231558) 

The All Terrain Tactical Enforcer was the main battle tank of the GAR.

 

The majority of the army's arsenal was constructed by [Rothana Heavy Engineering](/wiki/Rothana_Heavy_Engineering "Rothana Heavy Engineering"), which was a subsidiary of [Kuat Drive Yards](/wiki/Kuat_Drive_Yards "Kuat Drive Yards"), a company that had been opposed to the Confederacy for years by the start of the Clone Wars.[[31]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles-31) As the ground forces of the Republic military, the Grand Army used a wide range of vehicles to achieve various objectives. For [artillery](/wiki/Artillery "Artillery"), the Grand Army utilized the [AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannon](/wiki/AV-7_Anti-vehicle_Artillery_Cannon "AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannon"),[[126]](#cite_note-AV-7-126) the [Self-Propelled Heavy Artillery](/wiki/Self-Propelled_Heavy_Artillery "Self-Propelled Heavy Artillery") Turbolaser,[[127]](#cite_note-Heavy_Artillery-127) and the [Unstable Terrain Artillery Transport](/wiki/Unstable_Terrain_Artillery_Transport "Unstable Terrain Artillery Transport").[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3)

For transportation of clone troopers and cargo, the Grand Army utilized [AA-9 Freighter-Liners](/wiki/AA-9_Freighter-Liner "AA-9 Freighter-Liner") based on Coruscant.[[128]](#cite_note-Starfighters-128) Indeed, Grand Army forces were also deployed into operations by vehicles like the [Low Altitude Assault Transports](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport "Low Altitude Assault Transport")[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) and [*Nu*-class attack/transport shuttles](/wiki/Nu-class_attack/transport_shuttle "Nu-class attack/transport shuttle") of the Republic Navy.[[129]](#cite_note-Lair_of_G-129) The [*Jadthu*-class landing ship](/wiki/Jadthu-class_landing_ship "Jadthu-class landing ship"), too, would see use as a Republic lander.[[130]](#cite_note-Knights_of_Fate-130) The army also made use of several types of [speeders](/wiki/Speeder "Speeder"), including the BARC speeder,[[19]](#cite_note-BARC-19) the [74-Z speeder bike](/wiki/74-Z_speeder_bike "74-Z speeder bike"),[[131]](#cite_note-Starships_and_Speeders-131) the [CK-6 swoop bike](/wiki/CK-6_swoop_bike "CK-6 swoop bike"),[[132]](#cite_note-Databank_Freeco-132) and the [Infantry Support Platform](/wiki/Infantry_Support_Platform "Infantry Support Platform").[[133]](#cite_note-ISP_VE-133) Underwater operations made use of the [One Man Submersible Devilfish](/wiki/One_Man_Submersible_Devilfish "One Man Submersible Devilfish").[[106]](#cite_note-Water_War-106) A type of [sea ship](/wiki/Clone_sea_ship "Clone sea ship") also saw use during battles on the water.[[61]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_3-61)

 [![The All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport was used for missions like scouting, securing or patrolling territory, and frontline battles.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Cazne_ruins.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005171526) [![The All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport was used for missions like scouting, securing or patrolling territory, and frontline battles.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Cazne_ruins.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20121005171526)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Cazne_ruins.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005171526) 

The All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport was used for missions like scouting, securing or patrolling territory, and frontline battles.

 

The Republic's ground forces also used walkers, [repulsorcraft](/wiki/Repulsorcraft "Repulsorcraft"), and wheeled vehicles such as the [All Terrain Tactical Enforcer](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer"),[[18]](#cite_note-AT-TE-18) the [All Terrain Open Transport](/wiki/All_Terrain_Open_Transport "All Terrain Open Transport"),[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) the [All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport](/wiki/All_Terrain_Reconnaissance_Transport "All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport"),[[134]](#cite_note-AT-RT-134) the [All Terrain Armored Transport](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Transport "All Terrain Armored Transport"),[[135]](#cite_note-Last_Jedi_ICS-135) the [All Terrain Attack Pod](/wiki/All_Terrain_Attack_Pod "All Terrain Attack Pod"), the [Juggernaut A5](/wiki/Juggernaut_A5 "Juggernaut A5")[[136]](#cite_note-Republic_and_Separatist_Ships_(2)-136), the [HAVw A6 Juggernaut](/wiki/HAVw_A6_Juggernaut "HAVw A6 Juggernaut"),[[3]](#cite_note-Episode_III-3) the [TX-130 *Saber*-class fighter tank](/wiki/TX-130_Saber-class_fighter_tank "TX-130 Saber-class fighter tank"), the [RTT-04 armored troop transport](/wiki/RTT-04_armored_troop_transport "RTT-04 armored troop transport"),[[137]](#cite_note-Knights-137) and the [RX-200 *Falchion*-class assault tank](/wiki/RX-200_Falchion-class_assault_tank "RX-200 Falchion-class assault tank").[[138]](#cite_note-TZB-138) The [AT-FRC Force Reconnaissance Walker](/wiki/All_Terrain_Force_Reconnaissance_Walker "All Terrain Force Reconnaissance Walker") was used by ARC troopers for recon.[[139]](#cite_note-LbE-139)

## Weapons and equipment[]

:   "*Minimal destruction with blasters and droid poppers only. No rockets or detonators. Check your aim.*"
:   ―Cody[[105]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-105)

 [![The DC-15A blaster carbine was a standard-issue weapon that clone troopers used throughout the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Clones_maridun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110920040011) [![The DC-15A blaster carbine was a standard-issue weapon that clone troopers used throughout the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Clones_maridun.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110920040011)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Clones_maridun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110920040011) 

The DC-15A blaster carbine was a standard-issue weapon that clone troopers used throughout the Clone Wars.

 

For infantry weapons, the Grand Army of the Republic had a selection of [blasters](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster"), [grenades](/wiki/Grenade "Grenade"), and projectile launchers. For blasters, the army made use of the [DC-17 hand blaster](/wiki/DC-17_repeater_hand_blaster "DC-17 repeater hand blaster"),[[26]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-26) the [DC-17m blaster rifle](/wiki/DC-17m_Interchangeable_Weapon_System "DC-17m Interchangeable Weapon System"),[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) the [DC-15A blaster carbine](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_carbine "DC-15A blaster carbine"), the [DC-15A blaster rifle](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_rifle "DC-15A blaster rifle"),[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) the [DC-15LE](/wiki/DC-15LE "DC-15LE") blaster rifle, the [DC-15x sniper rifle](/wiki/DC-15x_sniper_rifle "DC-15x sniper rifle"),[[140]](#cite_note-Galactic_Defense-140) the [Z-6 rotary blaster cannon](/wiki/Z-6_rotary_blaster_cannon "Z-6 rotary blaster cannon"),[[118]](#cite_note-Ambush-118) the [BT X-42 heavy flame projector](/wiki/BT_X-42_heavy_flame_projector "BT X-42 heavy flame projector"),[[124]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-124) the [T-7 ion disruptor rifle](/wiki/T-7_ion_disruptor_rifle "T-7 ion disruptor rifle"),[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) the [DC-12U beam rifle](/wiki/DC-12U_beam_rifle "DC-12U beam rifle"),[[106]](#cite_note-Water_War-106)[[141]](#cite_note-Collapse-141) and the [Valken-38x](/wiki/Valken-38_blaster_rifle "Valken-38 blaster rifle") [sniper](/wiki/Sniper "Sniper").[[59]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-59) Also in use was the [773 Firepuncher rifle](/wiki/773_Firepuncher_sniper_rifle "773 Firepuncher sniper rifle"), which became a favorite of Republic snipers.[[78]](#cite_note-Join_the_Battle-78)

The [M3 Bulwark Blast Shield](/wiki/M3_Bulwark_Blast_Shield "M3 Bulwark Blast Shield") was a type of physical shield that could be worn by a clone trooper as a defensive barrier from enemy fire.[[122]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-122) [Clone riot troopers](/wiki/Riot_clone_trooper "Riot clone trooper") stationed on Coruscant wore a type of [riot shield](/wiki/Riot_shield "Riot shield"), which they wielded alongside a [baton](/wiki/Baton "Baton"), the [TZ-97 "Zapper" Shock Baton](/wiki/TZ-97_%22Zapper%22_Shock_Baton "TZ-97 \"Zapper\" Shock Baton"), in their policing actions.[[142]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-142)

 [![A type of heavy repeating blaster cannon operated by the Republic](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/RepublicEWeb.png/revision/latest?cb=20200225171031) [![A type of heavy repeating blaster cannon operated by the Republic](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/RepublicEWeb.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200225171031)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/RepublicEWeb.png/revision/latest?cb=20200225171031) 

A type of heavy repeating blaster cannon operated by the Republic

 

The types of grenades used were the [Class-A thermal detonator](/wiki/Class-A_thermal_detonator "Class-A thermal detonator"),[[86]](#cite_note-The_General-86) its [magnetic variant](/wiki/Magnetic_thermal_detonator "Magnetic thermal detonator"),[[143]](#cite_note-Weapons_F_at_Point_Rain-143) and the [N-20 Baradium-core thermal detonator](/wiki/N-20_Baradium-core_thermal_detonator "N-20 Baradium-core thermal detonator").[[144]](#cite_note-R2CH-144) Under the command of the Jedi, the Grand Army utilized [Electro Magnetic Pulse grenades](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse_grenade "Electromagnetic pulse grenade") to disable droids and other machines without risking organic collateral damage.[[105]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-105) For melee combat, the clones within the army uses [M8 combat knives](/wiki/M8_Combat_Knife "M8 Combat Knife") as simple melee weapons. The army utilized [ascension guns](/wiki/Ascension_gun "Ascension gun"),[[29]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-29) [mortars](/wiki/Clone_mortar "Clone mortar"),[[37]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-37) and [missile launchers](/wiki/Missile_launcher "Missile launcher"),[[118]](#cite_note-Ambush-118) such as the [RPS-6 rocket launcher](/wiki/RPS-6_rocket_launcher "RPS-6 rocket launcher")[[86]](#cite_note-The_General-86) and [RPC-2 Rocket Launcher](/wiki/RPC-2_Rocket_Launcher "RPC-2 Rocket Launcher").[[145]](#cite_note-On_the_Move-145) By the final days of the war, the [E-Web heavy repeating blaster cannons](/wiki/E-Web_heavy_repeating_blaster_cannon "E-Web heavy repeating blaster cannon") was used by the Republic,[[64]](#cite_note-Aftermath-64) with another [heavy repeating blaster](/wiki/Heavy_repeating_blaster "Heavy repeating blaster") also being used at earlier points.[[122]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-122)

## Behind the scenes[]

The Grand Army of the Republic first appeared in the [2002](/wiki/2002 "2002") film [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones"), the second installment of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy").[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) [LEGO](/wiki/LEGO "LEGO") introduced a [clone speeder](/wiki/Clone_speeder "Clone speeder") that has yet to appear in any [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") sources.[[146]](#cite_note-ShopPage-146)

[↑](#cite_ref-ten_years_53-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones") to [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). As the Grand Army of the Republic was established in *Attack of the Clones*, in must have been founded in 22 BBY. As the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") occurred in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY") per [Star Wars: On the Front Lines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_On_the_Front_Lines "Star Wars: On the Front Lines"), then ten [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") occurred between the Battle of Naboo and the founding of the GAR. 54.
